55        public void test0401() throws JavaScriptModelException {
56                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter" , "src", "test0401", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
57                ASTNode result = runConversion(sourceUnit, true);
58                ASTNode node = getASTNode((JavaScriptUnit) result, 0, 0);
59                assertNotNull(node);
60                assertTrue("Not a method declaration", node.getNodeType() == ASTNode.FUNCTION_DECLARATION); //$NON-NLS-1$
61                FunctionDeclaration methodDeclaration = (FunctionDeclaration) node;
62                Block block = methodDeclaration.getBody();
63                List statements = block.statements();
64                assertEquals("wrong size", 1, statements.size()); //$NON-NLS-1$
65                Statement statement = (Statement) statements.get(0);
66                assertTrue("Not a return statement", statement.getNodeType() == ASTNode.RETURN_STATEMENT); //$NON-NLS-1$
67                ReturnStatement returnStatement = (ReturnStatement) statement;
68                Expression expression = returnStatement.getExpression();
69                assertNotNull("there is no expression", expression); //$NON-NLS-1$
70                // call the default initialization
71                methodDeclaration.getReturnType();
72                ITypeBinding typeBinding = expression.resolveTypeBinding();
73                assertNotNull("No typebinding", typeBinding); //$NON-NLS-1$
74                assertEquals("wrong name", "int", typeBinding.getName()); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
75        }

281        /**
282         * http://dev.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=23162
283         */
284        public void test0409() throws JavaScriptModelException {
285                Hashtable options = JavaScriptCore.getOptions();
286                Hashtable newOptions = JavaScriptCore.getOptions();
287                try {
288                        newOptions.put(JavaScriptCore.COMPILER_SOURCE, JavaScriptCore.VERSION_1_4);
289                        JavaScriptCore.setOptions(newOptions);
290                        IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter" , "src", "test0409", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
291                        ASTNode result = runConversion(sourceUnit, true);
292                        assertTrue("Not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT); //$NON-NLS-1$
293                        JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) result; 
294                        assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 0);
295                        BindingsCollectorVisitor bindingsCollectorVisitor = new BindingsCollectorVisitor();
296                        compilationUnit.accept(bindingsCollectorVisitor);
297                        assertEquals("wrong number", 3, bindingsCollectorVisitor.getUnresolvedNodesSet().size()); //$NON-NLS-1$
298                        Map bindingsMap = bindingsCollectorVisitor.getBindingsMap();
299                        assertEquals("wrong number", 205, bindingsMap.size()); //$NON-NLS-1$
300                        ASTNodesCollectorVisitor nodesCollector = new ASTNodesCollectorVisitor();
301                        compilationUnit.accept(nodesCollector);
302                        Set detachedNodes = nodesCollector.getDetachedAstNodes();
303                        int counter = 0;
304                        for (Iterator iterator = detachedNodes.iterator(); iterator.hasNext(); ) {
305                                ASTNode detachedNode = (ASTNode) iterator.next();
306                                counter++;
307                                IBinding binding = (IBinding) bindingsMap.get(detachedNode);
308                                assertNotNull(binding);
309                                switch(detachedNode.getNodeType()) {
310                                        case ASTNode.ARRAY_ACCESS :
311                                        case ASTNode.ARRAY_CREATION :
312                                        case ASTNode.ARRAY_INITIALIZER :
313                                        case ASTNode.ASSIGNMENT :
314                                        case ASTNode.BOOLEAN_LITERAL :
315                                        case ASTNode.CAST_EXPRESSION :
316                                        case ASTNode.CHARACTER_LITERAL :
317                                        case ASTNode.CLASS_INSTANCE_CREATION :
318                                        case ASTNode.CONDITIONAL_EXPRESSION :
319                                        case ASTNode.FIELD_ACCESS :
320                                        case ASTNode.INFIX_EXPRESSION :
321                                        case ASTNode.INSTANCEOF_EXPRESSION :
322                                        case ASTNode.FUNCTION_INVOCATION :
323                                        case ASTNode.NULL_LITERAL :
324                                        case ASTNode.NUMBER_LITERAL :
325                                        case ASTNode.POSTFIX_EXPRESSION :
326                                        case ASTNode.PREFIX_EXPRESSION :
327                                        case ASTNode.THIS_EXPRESSION :
328                                        case ASTNode.TYPE_LITERAL :
329                                        case ASTNode.VARIABLE_DECLARATION_EXPRESSION :
330                                                ITypeBinding typeBinding = ((Expression) detachedNode).resolveTypeBinding();
331                                                if (!binding.equals(typeBinding)) {
332                                                        System.out.println(detachedNode);
333                                                }
334                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(typeBinding)); //$NON-NLS-1$
335                                                break;                                                
336                                        case ASTNode.VARIABLE_DECLARATION_FRAGMENT :
337                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(((VariableDeclarationFragment) detachedNode).resolveBinding())); //$NON-NLS-1$
338                                                break;                                                
339                                        case ASTNode.ANONYMOUS_CLASS_DECLARATION :
340                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(((AnonymousClassDeclaration) detachedNode).resolveBinding())); //$NON-NLS-1$
341                                                break;
342                                        case ASTNode.QUALIFIED_NAME :
343                                        case ASTNode.SIMPLE_NAME :
344                                                IBinding newBinding = ((Name) detachedNode).resolveBinding();
345                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(newBinding)); //$NON-NLS-1$
346                                                break;
347                                        case ASTNode.ARRAY_TYPE :
348                                        case ASTNode.SIMPLE_TYPE :
349                                        case ASTNode.PRIMITIVE_TYPE :
350                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(((Type) detachedNode).resolveBinding())); //$NON-NLS-1$
351                                                break;
352                                        case ASTNode.CONSTRUCTOR_INVOCATION :
353                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(((ConstructorInvocation) detachedNode).resolveConstructorBinding())); //$NON-NLS-1$
354                                                break;
355                                        case ASTNode.IMPORT_DECLARATION :
356                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(((ImportDeclaration) detachedNode).resolveBinding())); //$NON-NLS-1$
357                                                break;
358                                        case ASTNode.FUNCTION_DECLARATION :
359                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(((FunctionDeclaration) detachedNode).resolveBinding())); //$NON-NLS-1$
360                                                break;
361                                        case ASTNode.PACKAGE_DECLARATION :
362                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(((PackageDeclaration) detachedNode).resolveBinding())); //$NON-NLS-1$
363                                                break;
364                                        case ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION :
365                                                assertTrue("binding not equals", binding.equals(((TypeDeclaration) detachedNode).resolveBinding())); //$NON-NLS-1$
366                                                break;
367                                }
368                        }
369                } finally {
370                        JavaScriptCore.setOptions(options);
371                }
372        }

960                assertEquals("Not an expression statement", ASTNode.EXPRESSION_STATEMENT, node.getNodeType());

1114        public void test0440() throws JavaScriptModelException {
1115                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter" , "src", "test0440", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
1116                char[] source = sourceUnit.getSource().toCharArray();
1117                ASTNode result = runConversion(sourceUnit, true);
1118                assertTrue("not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT); //$NON-NLS-1$
1119                JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
1120                assertEquals("Wrong number of problems", 0, unit.getProblems().length); //$NON-NLS-1$<
1121                ASTNode node = getASTNode(unit, 0, 0, 0);
1122                assertEquals("Not a variable declaration statement", ASTNode.VARIABLE_DECLARATION_STATEMENT, node.getNodeType());
1123                VariableDeclarationStatement statement = (VariableDeclarationStatement) node;
1124                List fragments = statement.fragments();
1125                VariableDeclarationFragment fragment = (VariableDeclarationFragment) fragments.get(0);
1126                Expression expression = fragment.getInitializer();
1127                assertEquals("Not an infix expression", ASTNode.INFIX_EXPRESSION, expression.getNodeType());
1128                // 2 * 3 + "" + (true)
1129                InfixExpression infixExpression = (InfixExpression) expression;
1130                checkSourceRange(infixExpression, "2 * 3 + \"\" + (true)", source);
1131                Expression leftOperand = infixExpression.getLeftOperand();
1132                checkSourceRange(leftOperand, "2 * 3 + \"\"", source);
1133                checkSourceRange(infixExpression.getRightOperand(), "(true)", source);
1134                assertEquals("wrong operator", infixExpression.getOperator(), InfixExpression.Operator.PLUS);
1135                assertEquals("wrong type", ASTNode.INFIX_EXPRESSION, leftOperand.getNodeType());
1136                infixExpression = (InfixExpression) leftOperand;
1137                checkSourceRange(infixExpression, "2 * 3 + \"\"", source);
1138                leftOperand = infixExpression.getLeftOperand();
1139                checkSourceRange(leftOperand, "2 * 3", source);
1140                checkSourceRange(infixExpression.getRightOperand(), "\"\"", source);
1141                assertEquals("wrong operator", infixExpression.getOperator(), InfixExpression.Operator.PLUS);
1142                assertEquals("wrong type", ASTNode.INFIX_EXPRESSION, leftOperand.getNodeType());
1143                infixExpression = (InfixExpression) leftOperand;
1144                checkSourceRange(infixExpression, "2 * 3", source);
1145                leftOperand = infixExpression.getLeftOperand();
1146                checkSourceRange(leftOperand, "2", source);
1147                checkSourceRange(infixExpression.getRightOperand(), "3", source);
1148                assertEquals("wrong operator", infixExpression.getOperator(), InfixExpression.Operator.TIMES);
1149        }

1326        public void test0450() throws JavaScriptModelException {
1327                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter" , "src", "test0450", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
1328                ASTNode result = runConversion(sourceUnit, true);

1330                JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
1331                assertEquals("Wrong number of problems", 0, unit.getProblems().length); //$NON-NLS-1$
1332                ASTNode node = getASTNode(unit, 0);
1333                assertEquals("Not a type declaration", node.getNodeType(), ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION);
1334                TypeDeclaration typeDeclaration = (TypeDeclaration) node;
1335                ITypeBinding typeBinding = typeDeclaration.resolveBinding();
1336                assertNotNull("No type binding", typeBinding);
1337                assertTrue("not a class", typeBinding.isClass());
1338                assertTrue("not a toplevel type", typeBinding.isTopLevel());
1339                assertTrue("a local type", !typeBinding.isLocal());
1340                assertTrue("an anonymous type", !typeBinding.isAnonymous());
1341                assertTrue("a member type", !typeBinding.isMember());
1342                assertTrue("a nested type", !typeBinding.isNested());
1343                node = getASTNode(unit, 0, 0, 0);
1344                assertEquals("Not an expression statement", node.getNodeType(), ASTNode.EXPRESSION_STATEMENT);
1345                Expression expression = ((ExpressionStatement) node).getExpression();
1346                assertEquals("Not a class instance creation", expression.getNodeType(), ASTNode.CLASS_INSTANCE_CREATION);
1347                ClassInstanceCreation classInstanceCreation = (ClassInstanceCreation) expression;
1348                AnonymousClassDeclaration anonymousClassDeclaration = classInstanceCreation.getAnonymousClassDeclaration();
1349                typeBinding = anonymousClassDeclaration.resolveBinding();
1350                assertNotNull("No type binding", typeBinding);
1351                assertTrue("not a class", typeBinding.isClass());
1352                assertTrue("a toplevel type", !typeBinding.isTopLevel());
1353                assertTrue("not a local type", typeBinding.isLocal());
1354                assertTrue("not an anonymous type", typeBinding.isAnonymous());
1355                assertTrue("a member type", !typeBinding.isMember());
1356                assertTrue("not a nested type", typeBinding.isNested());
1357                ASTNode astNode = unit.findDeclaringNode(typeBinding);
1358                assertEquals("Wrong type", ASTNode.ANONYMOUS_CLASS_DECLARATION, astNode.getNodeType());
1359                assertNotNull("Didn't get a key", typeBinding.getKey());
1360                astNode = unit.findDeclaringNode(typeBinding.getKey());
1361                assertNotNull("Didn't get a declaring node", astNode);
1362                
1363                ITypeBinding typeBinding3 = classInstanceCreation.resolveTypeBinding();
1364                assertEquals("wrong binding", typeBinding, typeBinding3);
1365                
1366                List bodyDeclarations = anonymousClassDeclaration.bodyDeclarations();
1367                assertEquals("wrong size", 2, bodyDeclarations.size());
1368                BodyDeclaration bodyDeclaration = (BodyDeclaration) bodyDeclarations.get(0);
1369                assertTrue("not a type declaration", bodyDeclaration.getNodeType() == ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION);
1370                typeDeclaration = (TypeDeclaration) bodyDeclaration;
1371                
1372                bodyDeclaration = (BodyDeclaration) bodyDeclarations.get(1);
1373                FunctionDeclaration methodDeclaration = (FunctionDeclaration) bodyDeclaration;
1374                Block block = methodDeclaration.getBody();
1375                assertNotNull("No body", block);
1376                List statements = block.statements();
1377                assertEquals("wrong size", 2, statements.size());
1378                Statement statement = (Statement) statements.get(1);
1379                assertEquals("Not a variable declaration statement", statement.getNodeType(), ASTNode.VARIABLE_DECLARATION_STATEMENT);
1380                VariableDeclarationStatement variableDeclarationStatement = (VariableDeclarationStatement) statement;
1381                Type type = variableDeclarationStatement.getType();
1382                assertNotNull("No type", type);
1383                
1384                ITypeBinding typeBinding2 = type.resolveBinding();
1385                typeBinding = typeDeclaration.resolveBinding();
1386                assertTrue("not equals", typeBinding == typeBinding2);
1387                assertNotNull("No type binding", typeBinding);
1388                assertTrue("not a class", typeBinding.isClass());
1389                assertTrue("a toplevel type", !typeBinding.isTopLevel());
1390                assertTrue("an anonymous type", !typeBinding.isAnonymous());
1391                assertTrue("not a member type", typeBinding.isMember());
1392                assertTrue("not a nested type", typeBinding.isNested());                
1393                assertTrue("a local type", !typeBinding.isLocal());
1394                
1395                bodyDeclarations = typeDeclaration.bodyDeclarations();
1396                assertEquals("wrong size", 1, bodyDeclarations.size());
1397                bodyDeclaration = (BodyDeclaration) bodyDeclarations.get(0);
1398                assertTrue("not a type declaration", bodyDeclaration.getNodeType() == ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION);
1399                typeDeclaration = (TypeDeclaration) bodyDeclaration;
1400                typeBinding = typeDeclaration.resolveBinding();
1401                assertNotNull("No type binding", typeBinding);
1402                assertTrue("not a class", typeBinding.isClass());
1403                assertTrue("a toplevel type", !typeBinding.isTopLevel());
1404                assertTrue("an anonymous type", !typeBinding.isAnonymous());
1405                assertTrue("not a member type", typeBinding.isMember());
1406                assertTrue("not a nested type", typeBinding.isNested());                
1407                assertTrue("a local type", !typeBinding.isLocal());
1408        }

1640        public void test0461() throws JavaScriptModelException {
1641                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter" , "src", "test0461", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
1642                ASTNode result = runConversion(sourceUnit, false);
1643                char[] source = sourceUnit.getSource().toCharArray();
1644                assertTrue("not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT); //$NON-NLS-1$
1645                JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
1646                assertTrue("Has error", compilationUnit.getProblems().length == 0); //$NON-NLS-1$
1647                ASTNode node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0, 0, 0);
1648                assertNotNull("No node", node);
1649                assertTrue("Malformed", !isMalformed(node));
1650                assertTrue("not an expression statement", node.getNodeType() == ASTNode.EXPRESSION_STATEMENT); //$NON-NLS-1$
1651                ExpressionStatement expressionStatement = (ExpressionStatement) node;
1652                Expression expression = expressionStatement.getExpression();
1653                assertTrue("not an assignment", expression.getNodeType() == ASTNode.ASSIGNMENT); //$NON-NLS-1$
1654                Assignment assignment = (Assignment) expression;
1655                checkSourceRange(assignment, "z= foo().y.toList()", source);
1656                Expression expression2 = assignment.getRightHandSide();
1657                checkSourceRange(expression2, "foo().y.toList()", source);
1658                assertTrue("not a method invocation", expression2.getNodeType() == ASTNode.FUNCTION_INVOCATION);
1659                FunctionInvocation methodInvocation = (FunctionInvocation) expression2;
1660                Expression expression3 = methodInvocation.getExpression();
1661                checkSourceRange(expression3, "foo().y", source);
1662                checkSourceRange(methodInvocation.getName(), "toList", source);
1663                assertTrue("not a field access", expression3.getNodeType() == ASTNode.FIELD_ACCESS);
1664                FieldAccess fieldAccess = (FieldAccess) expression3;
1665                checkSourceRange(fieldAccess.getName(), "y", source);
1666                Expression expression4 = fieldAccess.getExpression();
1667                checkSourceRange(expression4, "foo()", source);
1668                assertTrue("not a method invocation", expression4.getNodeType() == ASTNode.FUNCTION_INVOCATION);
1669                FunctionInvocation methodInvocation2 = (FunctionInvocation) expression4;
1670                checkSourceRange(methodInvocation2.getName(), "foo", source);
1671                assertNull("no null", methodInvocation2.getExpression());
1672        }

1845                assertEquals("Wrong type", ASTNode.FIELD_DECLARATION, node.getNodeType());
1846                FieldDeclaration fieldDeclaration = (FieldDeclaration) node;
1847                List fragments = fieldDeclaration.fragments();
1848                assertEquals("wrong size", 1, fragments.size());
1849                VariableDeclarationFragment fragment = (VariableDeclarationFragment) fragments.get(0);
1850                
1851                ASTNode foundNode = compilationUnit.findDeclaringNode(variableBinding);
1852                assertNotNull("No found node", foundNode);
1853                assertEquals("wrong node", fragment, foundNode);
1854        }

2764        public void test0499() throws JavaScriptModelException {
2765                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter" , "src", "test0499", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
2766                ASTNode result = runConversion(sourceUnit, true);
2767                assertTrue("not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT); //$NON-NLS-1$
2768                JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
2769                assertEquals("Wrong number of problems", 1, unit.getProblems().length); //$NON-NLS-1$
2770                ASTNode node = getASTNode(unit, 0, 0, 1);
2771                assertNotNull(node);
2772                assertTrue("Not an expression statement", node.getNodeType() == ASTNode.EXPRESSION_STATEMENT); //$NON-NLS-1$
2773                Expression expression = ((ExpressionStatement) node).getExpression();
2774                assertTrue("Not an assignment", expression.getNodeType() == ASTNode.ASSIGNMENT); //$NON-NLS-1$
2775                Assignment assignment = (Assignment) expression;
2776                Expression expression2 = assignment.getRightHandSide();
2777                assertTrue("Not an infix expression", expression2.getNodeType() == ASTNode.INFIX_EXPRESSION); //$NON-NLS-1$
2778                InfixExpression infixExpression = (InfixExpression) expression2;
2779                Expression expression3 = infixExpression.getLeftOperand();
2780                assertTrue("Not a simple name", expression3.getNodeType() == ASTNode.SIMPLE_NAME); //$NON-NLS-1$
2781                ITypeBinding binding = expression3.resolveTypeBinding();
2782                assertNotNull("No binding", binding);
2783                Expression expression4 = assignment.getLeftHandSide();
2784                assertTrue("Not a simple name", expression4.getNodeType() == ASTNode.SIMPLE_NAME); //$NON-NLS-1$
2785                ITypeBinding binding2 = expression4.resolveTypeBinding();
2786                assertNotNull("No binding", binding2);
2787                assertTrue("Should be the same", binding == binding2);
2788        }

2796        public void test0500() throws JavaScriptModelException {
2797                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter" , "src", "test0500", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
2798                IJavaScriptProject project = sourceUnit.getJavaScriptProject();
2799                Map originalOptions = project.getOptions(false);
2800                try {
2801                        project.setOption(JavaScriptCore.COMPILER_PB_INVALID_JAVADOC, JavaScriptCore.ERROR);
2802                        project.setOption(JavaScriptCore.COMPILER_PB_MISSING_JAVADOC_TAGS, JavaScriptCore.ERROR);
2803                        project.setOption(JavaScriptCore.COMPILER_PB_MISSING_JAVADOC_COMMENTS, JavaScriptCore.ERROR);
2804                        JavaScriptUnit result = (JavaScriptUnit)runConversion(sourceUnit, true);
2805                        IProblem[] problems= result.getProblems();
2806                        assertTrue(problems.length == 1);
2807                        assertEquals("Invalid warning", "Javadoc: Missing tag for parameter a", problems[0].getMessage());
2808                } finally {
2809                        project.setOptions(originalOptions);
2810                }
2811        }

3336        public void test0516() throws JavaScriptModelException {
3337                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter", "src", "test0516", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
3338                char[] source = sourceUnit.getSource().toCharArray();
3339                ASTNode result = runConversion(sourceUnit, false);
3340                final JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
3341                assertEquals("Wrong number of problems", 0, unit.getProblems().length); //$NON-NLS-1$
3342                ASTNode node = getASTNode(unit, 0, 0);
3343                assertNotNull("No node", node);
3344                assertTrue("not a method declaration", node.getNodeType() == ASTNode.FUNCTION_DECLARATION);
3345                FunctionDeclaration declaration = (FunctionDeclaration) node;
3346                ASTParser parser = ASTParser.newParser(AST.JLS2);
3347                parser.setKind(ASTParser.K_CLASS_BODY_DECLARATIONS);
3348                parser.setSource(source);
3349                parser.setSourceRange(declaration.getStartPosition(), declaration.getLength());
3350                parser.setCompilerOptions(JavaScriptCore.getOptions());
3351                ASTNode result2 = parser.createAST(null);
3352                assertNotNull("No node", result2);
3353                assertTrue("not a type declaration", result2.getNodeType() == ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION);
3354                TypeDeclaration typeDeclaration = (TypeDeclaration) result2;
3355                List bodyDeclarations = typeDeclaration.bodyDeclarations();
3356                assertEquals("wrong size", 1, bodyDeclarations.size());
3357                BodyDeclaration bodyDeclaration = (BodyDeclaration) bodyDeclarations.get(0);
3358                assertTrue(declaration.subtreeMatch(new ASTMatcher(), bodyDeclaration));
3359                ASTNode root = bodyDeclaration.getRoot();
3360                assertNotNull("No root", root);
3361                assertTrue("not a compilation unit", root.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT);
3362                JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) root;
3363                assertEquals("wrong problem size", 0, compilationUnit.getProblems().length);
3364                assertNotNull("No comments", compilationUnit.getCommentList());
3365                assertEquals("Wrong size", 3, compilationUnit.getCommentList().size());
3366        }

3509        /**
3510         * Ensure an OperationCanceledException is correcly thrown when progress monitor is canceled
3511         * @deprecated using deprecated code
3512         */
3513        public void test0521() throws JavaScriptModelException {
3514                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter", "src", "test0521", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
3515                
3516                // count the number of time isCanceled() is called when converting this source unit
3517                WorkingCopyOwner owner = new WorkingCopyOwner() {};
3518                CancelCounter counter = new CancelCounter();
3519                ASTParser parser = ASTParser.newParser(AST.JLS2);
3520                parser.setSource(sourceUnit);
3521                parser.setResolveBindings(true);
3522                parser.setWorkingCopyOwner(owner);
3523                parser.createAST(counter);
3524                
3525                // throw an OperatonCanceledException at each point isCanceled() is called
3526                for (int i = 0; i < counter.count; i++) {
3527                        boolean gotException = false;
3528                        try {
3529                                parser = ASTParser.newParser(AST.JLS2);
3530                                parser.setSource(sourceUnit);
3531                                parser.setResolveBindings(true);
3532                                parser.setWorkingCopyOwner(owner);
3533                                parser.createAST(new Canceler(i));
3534                        } catch (OperationCanceledException e) {
3535                                gotException = true;
3536                        }
3537                        assertTrue("Should get an OperationCanceledException (" + i + ")", gotException);
3538                }
3539                
3540                // last should not throw an OperationCanceledException
3541                parser = ASTParser.newParser(AST.JLS2);
3542                parser.setSource(sourceUnit);
3543                parser.setResolveBindings(true);
3544                parser.setWorkingCopyOwner(owner);
3545                parser.createAST(new Canceler(counter.count));
3546        }

3551        public void test0522() throws JavaScriptModelException {

3553                assertNotNull(classFile);

3558                assertNotNull(methods);
3559                assertEquals("wrong size", 2, methods.length);
3560                IFunction method = methods[1];
3561                ISourceRange sourceRange = method.getSourceRange(); 
3562                ASTNode result = runConversion(classFile, sourceRange.getOffset() + sourceRange.getLength() / 2, true);
3563                assertNotNull(result);
3564                assertTrue("Not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT); //$NON-NLS-1$
3565                ASTNode node = getASTNode((JavaScriptUnit) result, 1, 0);
3566                assertTrue("Not a method declaration", node.getNodeType() == ASTNode.FUNCTION_DECLARATION); //$NON-NLS-1$
3567                FunctionDeclaration methodDeclaration = (FunctionDeclaration) node;
3568                assertEquals("wrong name", "test", methodDeclaration.getName().getIdentifier());
3569                IFunctionBinding methodBinding = methodDeclaration.resolveBinding();
3570                assertNotNull(methodBinding);
3571                List statements = ((FunctionDeclaration) node).getBody().statements();
3572                assertEquals("wrong size", 2, statements.size());
3573                ASTNode node2 = (ASTNode) statements.get(1);
3574                assertNotNull(node2);

3577                Expression expression = expressionStatement.getExpression();
3578                assertTrue("Not a method invocation", expression.getNodeType() == ASTNode.FUNCTION_INVOCATION); //$NON-NLS-1$
3579                FunctionInvocation methodInvocation = (FunctionInvocation) expression;
3580                Expression expression2 = methodInvocation.getExpression();
3581                assertTrue("Not a simple name", expression2.getNodeType() == ASTNode.SIMPLE_NAME); //$NON-NLS-1$
3582                SimpleName simpleName = (SimpleName) expression2;
3583                IBinding binding  = simpleName.resolveBinding();
3584                assertNotNull("No binding", binding); //$NON-NLS-1$
3585                assertTrue("wrong type", binding.getKind() == IBinding.VARIABLE); //$NON-NLS-1$
3586                IVariableBinding variableBinding = (IVariableBinding) binding;
3587                assertEquals("Wrong name", "a", variableBinding.getName()); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
3588                SimpleName simpleName2 = methodInvocation.getName();
3589                assertEquals("Wrong name", "clone", simpleName2.getIdentifier()); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
3590                IBinding binding2 = simpleName2.resolveBinding();
3591                assertNotNull("no binding2", binding2); //$NON-NLS-1$
3592                assertTrue("Wrong type", binding2.getKind() == IBinding.METHOD); //$NON-NLS-1$
3593                IFunctionBinding methodBinding2 = (IFunctionBinding) binding2;
3594                assertEquals("Wrong name", "clone", methodBinding2.getName()); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$

4386        /**
4387         * https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=56697
4388         */
4389        public void test0541() throws JavaScriptModelException {
4390                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter", "src", "test0541", "A.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
4391                ASTNode result = runConversion(sourceUnit, true);
4392                final JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
4393                assertEquals("Wrong number of problems", 0, unit.getProblems().length); //$NON-NLS-1$
4394                ASTNode node = getASTNode(unit, 0, 0);
4395                assertEquals("not a field declaration", ASTNode.FIELD_DECLARATION, node.getNodeType());
4396                class Change14FieldAccessASTVisitor extends ASTVisitor {
4397                        int counter;
4398                        Change14FieldAccessASTVisitor() {
4399                                counter = 0;
4400                        }
4401                        public void endVisit(QualifiedName qualifiedName) {
4402                                IBinding i_binding = qualifiedName.getQualifier().resolveBinding();                                                
4403                                ITypeBinding type_binding = qualifiedName.getQualifier().resolveTypeBinding();
4404                                if (i_binding == null || type_binding == null) {
4405                                        counter++;
4406                                }
4407                        }
4408                }
4409                Change14FieldAccessASTVisitor visitor = new Change14FieldAccessASTVisitor();

4769        public void test0552() throws JavaScriptModelException {
4770                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter", "src", "test0552", "Test.js");
4771                char[] source = sourceUnit.getSource().toCharArray();
4772                JavaScriptUnit result = (JavaScriptUnit) runConversion(sourceUnit, true);
4773                assertEquals("Got errors", 0, result.getProblems().length);
4774                TypeDeclaration declaration = (TypeDeclaration) result.types().get(0);
4775                Block body = declaration.getMethods()[0].getBody();
4776                ExpressionStatement expr = (ExpressionStatement) body.statements().get(0);
4777                FunctionInvocation invocation = (FunctionInvocation) expr.getExpression();
4778                InfixExpression node = (InfixExpression) invocation.arguments().get(0);
4779                ITypeBinding typeBinding = node.resolveTypeBinding();
4780                assertEquals("wrong type", "java.lang.String", typeBinding.getQualifiedName());
4781                checkSourceRange(node, "\"a\" + \"a\" + \"a\"", source);
4782                List extendedOperands = node.extendedOperands();
4783                assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, extendedOperands.size());
4784                Expression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
4785                checkSourceRange(leftOperand, "\"a\"", source);
4786                typeBinding = leftOperand.resolveTypeBinding();
4787                assertEquals("wrong type", "java.lang.String", typeBinding.getQualifiedName());
4788                Expression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
4789                checkSourceRange(rightOperand, "\"a\"", source);
4790                typeBinding = rightOperand.resolveTypeBinding();
4791                assertEquals("wrong type", "java.lang.String", typeBinding.getQualifiedName());
4792                Expression expression = (Expression) extendedOperands.get(0);
4793                checkSourceRange(expression, "\"a\"", source);
4794                typeBinding = expression.resolveTypeBinding();
4795                assertEquals("wrong type", "java.lang.String", typeBinding.getQualifiedName());
4796        }

5053                ParenthesizedExpression parenthesizedExpression = (ParenthesizedExpression) expression3;
5054                Expression expression4 = parenthesizedExpression.getExpression();
5055                assertEquals("Wrong type", ASTNode.STRING_LITERAL, expression4.getNodeType());
5056                checkSourceRange(expression4, "\" \"", source);
5057        }

5176        public void test0569() throws JavaScriptModelException {

5194                node = getASTNode(unit, 0, 0);

5202         * Ensures that the type binding from an import and the type binding from a type ref are equals
5203         * when the AST is computed using IJavaScriptUnit#reconcile(...)
5204         * (regression test for bug 83210 Unidentical ITypeBindings for same type from same AST from reconcile)
5205         */
5206        public void test0570() throws CoreException {
5207                IJavaScriptUnit workingCopy = null;
5208                try {
5209                        workingCopy = getWorkingCopy("/Converter/src/X.js", true);
5210                        JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) buildAST(
5211                                "import java.util.List;\n" +
5212                                "public class X{\n" +
5213                                "  List field;\n" +
5214                                "}",
5215                                workingCopy
5216                        );
5217                        ImportDeclaration importDeclaration = (ImportDeclaration) unit.imports().iterator().next();
5218                        TypeDeclaration typeDeclaration = (TypeDeclaration) unit.types().iterator().next();
5219                        FieldDeclaration fieldDeclaration = typeDeclaration.getFields()[0];
5220                        Type type = fieldDeclaration.getType();
5221                        IBinding importBinding = importDeclaration.resolveBinding();
5222                        IBinding typeBinding = type.resolveBinding();
5223                        assertEquals(importBinding,typeBinding);
5224                } finally {
5225                        if (workingCopy != null)
5226                                workingCopy.discardWorkingCopy();
5227                }
5228        }

5405                                true/*resolve*/);
5406                        FunctionDeclaration method = (FunctionDeclaration) buildAST(workingCopy);
